P1903 The numGlyphs value equals the number of entries in the loca array plus one numGlyphs = 1224
W1900 maxSizeOfInstructions computation not via either approved method glyf maxSizeOfInstructions=401, prep size=239, fpgm size=3596, whereas maxp maxSizeOfInstruction is 3596
